  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A','$B']],-->,M],T]],[[['{...}',['$B']],-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])

  (|- 
    ( ( { $A $B } --> $M) $T)) 
          ( ( { $B } --> $M) 
                (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[['M',-->,[['[...]',['$A','$B']]]],T]],[['M',-->,[['[...]',['$A']]]],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])

    ( (M --> 
        ( [ $A $B ])) $T)) 
            ( (M --> 
                ( [ $A ])) 
                    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))

  (|- 
    ( (M -->
